<pr_description>
Goodwe goodwe-wifi-et: unsupported decode "float32"
### Describe the bug

After updating EVCC to the newly released version `v0.304.0`, the Goodwe integration fails to initialize during startup. The system throws a fatal error specifically related to the `goodwe-wifi-et` template, stating that `aa55udp` has an unsupported decode for `"float32"`. This causes the site to fail booting due to a missing grid meter instance.

### Steps to reproduce

1. Update EVCC to version `v0.304.0`.
2. Configure a grid meter using the `goodwe-wifi-et` template.
3. Start the EVCC service.
4. The system fails to start and displays the unsupported decode `"float32"` error in the UI and logs.

### Configuration details

```yaml
site:
  meters:
    grid: my_grid
    pv: my_pv
    battery: my_battery
....
meters:
  - name: my_grid
    type: template
    template: goodwe-wifi-et
    usage: grid
    host: 192.168.1.26 # IP address or hostname, IP address of the inverter (port 8899)
  - name: my_pv
    type: template
    template: goodwe-wifi-et
    usage: pv
    host: 192.168.1.26 # IP address or hostname, IP address of the inverter (port 8899)
  - name: my_battery
    type: template
    template: goodwe-wifi-et
    usage: battery
    host: 192.168.1.26 # IP address or hostname, IP address of the inverter (port 8899)
...
```

### Log details

```text
[main  ] FATAL 2026/04/02 15:07:50 meter [my_grid] cannot create meter 'my_grid': cannot create meter type 'template:goodwe-wifi-et': cannot create meter type 'custom': energy: aa55udp: unsupported decode "float32" (want int32be|uint32be|int16be|uint16be)
failed booting site: missing grid meter instance
```

### What type of operating system or environment does evcc run on?

HomeAssistant Add-on

### External automation

- [x] I have made sure that no external automation like HomeAssistant or Node-RED is active or accessing any of the mentioned devices when this issue occurs.

### Nightly build

- [x] I have verified that the issue is reproducible with the latest nightly build

### Version

0.304.0

     1	package plugin
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"
     5	        "encoding/binary"
     6	        "encoding/hex"
     7	        "errors"
     8	        "fmt"
     9	        "net"
    10	        "strings"
    11	        "time"
    12	
    13	        "github.com/evcc-io/evcc/util"
    14	)
    15	
    16	// AA55UDP implements the GoodWe WiFi AA55-over-UDP wire protocol as a generic
    17	// evcc source plugin.
    18	//
    19	// The inverter speaks a simple request/response protocol over UDP port 8899:
    20	//
    21	//      Request:  [6-byte Modbus PDU body] [Modbus CRC-16, little-endian]
    22	//      Response: AA 55 [src] 03 [byteCount] [payload…] [CRC]
    23	//
    24	// src varies by inverter family (0x7F for DT/DNS, 0xF7 for ET/EH/BT/BH);
    25	// only the AA 55 magic bytes and function code 0x03 are validated.
    26	//
    27	// Each instance reads exactly one value from one register (or register pair
    28	// for 32-bit values), matching how Modbus source plugins work.  The PDU is
    29	// constructed from register and count; the decoded value is always at offset 0
    30	// of the response payload.
    31	type AA55UDP struct {
    32	        log    *util.Logger
    33	        conn   *net.UDPConn
    34	        pdu    []byte // 6-byte PDU body, no CRC
    35	        decode string // int32be | uint32be | int16be | uint16be
    36	        scale  float64
    37	}
    38	
    39	func init() {
    40	        registry.AddCtx("aa55udp", NewAA55UDPFromConfig)
    41	}
    42	
    43	// NewAA55UDPFromConfig creates an AA55UDP plugin from a source block:
    44	//
    45	//      source:   aa55udp
    46	//      host:     192.168.1.26   # inverter IP; port 8899 is always used
    47	//      register: 30127          # Modbus register address (0-based, uint16)
    48	//      count:    2              # number of registers to read (1=U16, 2=S32/U32)
    49	//      decode:   int32be        # int32be | uint32be | int16be | uint16be
    50	//      scale:    1.0            # optional multiplier (default 1.0)
    51	func NewAA55UDPFromConfig(_ context.Context, other map[string]interface{}) (Plugin, error) {
    52	        cc := struct {
    53	                Host     string  `mapstructure:"host"`
    54	                Register uint16  `mapstructure:"register"`
    55	                Count    uint16  `mapstructure:"count"`
    56	                Decode   string  `mapstructure:"decode"`
    57	                Scale    float64 `mapstructure:"scale"`
    58	        }{
    59	                Count: 2,
    60	                Scale: 1.0,
    61	        }
    62	        if err := util.DecodeOther(other, &cc); err != nil {
    63	                return nil, err
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if cc.Count == 0 {
    67	                return nil, errors.New("aa55udp: count must be ≥ 1")
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        switch cc.Decode {
    71	        case "int32be", "uint32be", "int16be", "uint16be":
    72	        default:
    73	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: unsupported decode %q (want int32be|uint32be|int16be|uint16be)", cc.Decode)
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        pdu := buildPDU(cc.Register, cc.Count)
    77	
    78	        addr, err := net.ResolveUDPAddr("udp4", net.JoinHostPort(cc.Host, "8899"))
    79	        if err != nil {
    80	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: resolve %s: %w", cc.Host, err)
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        conn, err := net.DialUDP("udp4", nil, addr)
    84	        if err != nil {
    85	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: dial %s: %w", cc.Host, err)
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        return &AA55UDP{
    89	                log:    util.NewLogger("aa55udp"),
    90	                conn:   conn,
    91	                pdu:    pdu,
    92	                decode: cc.Decode,
    93	                scale:  cc.Scale,
    94	        }, nil
    95	}
    96	
    97	// FloatGetter implements the evcc Plugin interface.
    98	func (p *AA55UDP) FloatGetter() (func() (float64, error), error) {
    99	        return p.query, nil
   100	}
   101	
   102	// query sends the PDU and returns the decoded, scaled value at offset 0 of the
   103	// response payload.
   104	func (p *AA55UDP) query() (float64, error) {
   105	        packet := append(p.pdu, modbusCRC16(p.pdu)...)
   106	
   107	        if _, err := p.conn.Write(packet); err != nil {
   108	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp write: %w", err)
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        if err := p.conn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(4 * time.Second)); err != nil {
   112	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp deadline: %w", err)
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        buf := make([]byte, 512)
   116	        n, err := p.conn.Read(buf)
   117	        if err != nil {
   118	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp read: %w", err)
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        payload, err := stripAA55Header(buf[:n])
   122	        if err != nil {
   123	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: %w", err)
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        v, err := decodeAt(payload, 0, p.decode)
   127	        if err != nil {
   128	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: %w", err)
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        return v * p.scale, nil
   132	}
   133	
   134	// aa55InverterAddr is the target address byte used in all AA55 request PDUs.
   135	// The GoodWe WiFi module always uses 0x7F as the inverter target address,
   136	// regardless of inverter family. The family only affects the source byte in
   137	// responses (0x7F for DT/DNS, 0xF7 for ET/EH/BT/BH).
   138	const aa55InverterAddr = 0x7F
   139	
   140	// aa55ReadFunc is the Modbus function code for READ HOLDING REGISTERS.
   141	const aa55ReadFunc = 0x03
   142	
   143	// buildPDU constructs the 6-byte Modbus PDU body for a READ HOLDING REGISTERS
   144	// request targeting the GoodWe WiFi module.
   145	func buildPDU(register, count uint16) []byte {
   146	        return []byte{
   147	                aa55InverterAddr, aa55ReadFunc,
   148	                byte(register >> 8), byte(register),
   149	                byte(count >> 8), byte(count),
   150	        }
   151	}
   152	
   153	// parsePDUHex decodes a hex string (spaces allowed) into exactly 6 bytes.
   154	// Kept for use in tests.
   155	func parsePDUHex(s string) ([]byte, error) {
   156	        clean := strings.ReplaceAll(s, " ", "")
   157	        b, err := hex.DecodeString(clean)
   158	        if err != nil {
   159	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: invalid pdu %q: %w", s, err)
   160	        }
   161	        if len(b) != 6 {
   162	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: pdu must be 6 bytes, got %d", len(b))
   163	        }
   164	        return b, nil
   165	}
   166	
   167	// stripAA55Header validates the AA55 response frame and returns the bare
   168	// payload (without the 5-byte header and trailing 2-byte CRC).
   169	// buf[2] is the inverter source address and varies by family — only the
   170	// AA 55 magic bytes and function code 0x03 are validated.
   171	func stripAA55Header(buf []byte) ([]byte, error) {
   172	        if len(buf) < 6 || buf[0] != 0xAA || buf[1] != 0x55 || buf[3] != 0x03 {
   173	                return nil, errors.New("invalid response header")
   174	        }
   175	        byteCount := int(buf[4])
   176	        if len(buf) < 5+byteCount+2 {
   177	                return nil, errors.New("short response")
   178	        }
   179	        return buf[5 : 5+byteCount], nil
   180	}
   181	
   182	// decodeAt extracts an integer at the given byte offset of payload and
   183	// interprets it according to decode.
   184	func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
   185	        switch decode {
   186	        case "int32be":
   187	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   188	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   189	                }
   190	                return float64(int32(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))), nil
   191	        case "uint32be":
   192	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   193	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   194	                }
   195	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:])), nil
   196	        case "int16be":
   197	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   198	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   199	                }
   200	                return float64(int16(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:]))), nil
   201	        case "uint16be":
   202	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   203	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   204	                }
   205	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
   206	        }
   207	        return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode type: %s", decode)
   208	}
   209	
   210	// modbusCRC16 computes the Modbus CRC-16 (little-endian byte order).
   211	func modbusCRC16(data []byte) []byte {
   212	        crc := uint16(0xFFFF)
   213	        for _, b := range data {
   214	                crc ^= uint16(b)
   215	                for i := 0; i < 8; i++ {
   216	                        if crc&0x0001 != 0 {
   217	                                crc = (crc >> 1) ^ 0xA001
   218	                        } else {
   219	                                crc >>= 1
   220	                        }
   221	                }
   222	        }
   223	        return []byte{byte(crc & 0xFF), byte(crc >> 8)}
   224	}

    63	func TestBuildPDU_DTpower(t *testing.T) {
    64	        // DT power: register 0x75AF, count 2 → READ 2 @ 0x75AF
    65	        got := buildPDU(0x75AF, 2)
    66	        assert.Equal(t, []byte{0x7f, 0x03, 0x75, 0xaf, 0x00, 0x02}, got)
    67	}

    70	        // ET grid: register 0x8943, count 2

    72	        assert.Equal(t, []byte{0x7f, 0x03, 0x89, 0x43, 0x00, 0x02}, got)

    75	func TestBuildPDU_SoC(t *testing.T) {
    76	        // ET SoC: register 0x908F, count 1 (U16)
    77	        got := buildPDU(0x908F, 1)
    78	        assert.Equal(t, []byte{0x7f, 0x03, 0x90, 0x8f, 0x00, 0x01}, got)
    79	}

   166	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   167	// modbusCRC16 tests
   168	// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   169	
   170	func TestModbusCRC16_DTPdu(t *testing.T) {
   171	        // DT power PDU 7f 03 75 af 00 02 → CRC d1 ba
   172	        pdu := buildPDU(0x75AF, 2)
   173	        crc := modbusCRC16(pdu)
   174	        // Verify round-trip: CRC is 2 bytes and deterministic
   175	        assert.Len(t, crc, 2)
   176	        assert.Equal(t, crc, modbusCRC16(pdu), "CRC must be deterministic")
   177	}
   178	
   179	func TestModbusCRC16_ETPdu(t *testing.T) {
   180	        // ET grid PDU 7f 03 89 43 00 02 → CRC is 2 bytes
   181	        pdu := buildPDU(0x8943, 2)
   182	        crc := modbusCRC16(pdu)
   183	        assert.Len(t, crc, 2)
   184	        assert.Equal(t, crc, modbusCRC16(pdu))
   185	}
   186	
   187	func TestModbusCRC16_KnownValue(t *testing.T) {
   188	        // The original block-read DT PDU 7f 03 75 94 00 49 → CRC d5 c2
   189	        // This is a known-good value verified against real hardware.
   190	        pdu, err := parsePDUHex("7f0375940049")
   191	        require.NoError(t, err)
   192	        assert.Equal(t, []byte{0xd5, 0xc2}, modbusCRC16(pdu))
   193	}

   276	// TestFloatGetter_DT_Power verifies the full query/decode pipeline using the

   278	func TestFloatGetter_DT_Power(t *testing.T) {

   365	// Test helpers

   367	
   368	func mustHex(t *testing.T, s string) []byte {
   369	        t.Helper()
   370	        b, err := hex.DecodeString(s)
   371	        require.NoError(t, err)
   372	        return b
   373	}
   374	
   375	// assertBlockOffset extracts bytes at offset within a block-read capture and
   376	// asserts the decoded value matches expected.  This verifies that the register
   377	// address arithmetic is correct: the bytes the inverter would return for a
   378	// single-register read are identical to the bytes at the register's offset
   379	// within the block.
   380	func assertBlockOffset(t *testing.T, capHex string, offset int, decode string, scale, expected float64) {
   381	        t.Helper()
   382	        payload, err := stripAA55Header(mustHex(t, capHex))
   383	        require.NoError(t, err)
   384	        v, err := decodeAt(payload, offset, decode)
   385	        require.NoError(t, err)
   386	        assert.InDelta(t, expected, v*scale, 0.05)
   387	}

    15	// Register contains the ModBus register configuration
    16	type Register struct {
    17	        Address  uint16 // Length  uint16
    18	        Type     string
    19	        Decode   string // TODO deprecated, use Encoding
    20	        Encoding string
    21	        BitMask  string
    22	}
    23	
    24	func (r Register) Error() error {
    25	        if r.Type == "" {
    26	                return errors.New("type is required")
    27	        }
    28	        if r.Decode == "" && r.Encoding == "" {
    29	                return errors.New("encoding is required")
    30	        }
    31	        if r.Decode != "" && r.Encoding != "" {
    32	                return errors.New("must not have decide when encoding is specified")
    33	        }
    34	        return nil
    35	}
    36	
    37	func (r Register) encoding() string {
    38	        if r.Encoding != "" {
    39	                return r.Encoding
    40	        }
    41	        return r.Decode
    42	}
    43	
    44	func (r Register) Length() (uint16, error) {
    45	        enc := r.encoding()
    46	        switch {
    47	        case strings.Contains(enc, "8") || strings.Contains(enc, "16"):
    48	                return 1, nil
    49	        case strings.Contains(enc, "32") || strings.Contains(enc, "754"):
    50	                return 2, nil
    51	        case strings.Contains(enc, "64"):
    52	                return 4, nil
    53	        case strings.EqualFold(enc, "bytes"):
    54	                return 0, nil
    55	        default:
    56	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("invalid register length: %s", enc)
    57	        }
    58	}
    59	
    60	func (r Register) FuncCode() (uint8, error) {
    61	        switch strings.ToLower(r.Type) {
    62	        case "holding":
    63	                return modbus.FuncCodeReadHoldingRegisters, nil
    64	        case "input":
    65	                return modbus.FuncCodeReadInputRegisters, nil
    66	        case "coil":
    67	                return modbus.FuncCodeReadCoils, nil
    68	        case "writesingle", "writeholding":
    69	                return modbus.FuncCodeWriteSingleRegister, nil
    70	        case "writemultiple", "writeholdings":
    71	                return modbus.FuncCodeWriteMultipleRegisters, nil
    72	        case "writecoil":
    73	                return modbus.FuncCodeWriteSingleCoil, nil
    74	        default:
    75	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("invalid register type: %s", r.Type)
    76	        }
    77	}
    78	
    79	func (r Register) DecodeFunc() (func([]byte) float64, error) {
    80	        switch strings.ToLower(r.encoding()) {
    81	        // 8 bit (coil)
    82	        case "bool8":
    83	                return decodeBool8, nil
    84	
    85	        // 16 bit
    86	        case "int16":
    87	                return asFloat64(encoding.Int16), nil
    88	        case "int16nan":
    89	                return decodeNaN16(asFloat64(encoding.Int16), 1<<15, 1<<15-1), nil
    90	        case "uint16":
    91	                return asFloat64(encoding.Uint16), nil
    92	        case "uint16nan":
    93	                return decodeNaN16(asFloat64(encoding.Uint16), 1<<16-1), nil
    94	        case "bool16":
    95	                mask, err := decodeMask(r.BitMask)
    96	                if err != nil {
    97	                        return nil, err
    98	                }
    99	                return decodeBool16(mask), nil
   100	
   101	        // 32 bit
   102	        case "int32":
   103	                return asFloat64(encoding.Int32), nil
   104	        case "int32nan":
   105	                return decodeNaN32(asFloat64(encoding.Int32), 1<<31, 1<<31-1), nil
   106	        case "int32s":
   107	                return asFloat64(encoding.Int32LswFirst), nil
   108	        case "uint32":
   109	                return asFloat64(encoding.Uint32), nil
   110	        case "uint32s":
   111	                return asFloat64(encoding.Uint32LswFirst), nil
   112	        case "uint32nan":
   113	                return decodeNaN32(asFloat64(encoding.Uint32), 1<<32-1), nil
   114	        case "float32", "ieee754":
   115	                return asFloat64(encoding.Float32), nil
   116	        case "float32s", "ieee754s":
   117	                return asFloat64(encoding.Float32LswFirst), nil
   118	        case "float32nans":
   119	                return decodeNaN32(asFloat64(encoding.Float32LswFirst), 0xffffff7f), nil
   120	
   121	        // 64 bit
   122	        case "int64":
   123	                return asFloat64(encoding.Int64), nil
   124	        case "uint64":
   125	                return asFloat64(encoding.Uint64), nil
   126	        case "uint64nan":
   127	                return decodeNaN64(asFloat64(encoding.Uint64), 1<<64-1), nil
   128	        case "float64":
   129	                return encoding.Float64, nil
   130	
   131	        default:
   132	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid register decoding: %s", r.encoding())
   133	        }
   134	}
   135	
   136	func (r Register) encodeToBytes(fun func(float64) uint64) (func(float64) ([]byte, error), error) {
   137	        length, err := r.Length()
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return nil, err
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        // swapped
   143	        if strings.HasSuffix(strings.ToLower(r.encoding()), "s") {
   144	                if length != 2 {
   145	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid swapped encoding register length: %d", length)
   146	                }
   147	
   148	                inner := fun
   149	                fun = func(f float64) uint64 {
   150	                        v := inner(f)
   151	                        return v&0xFFFF<<16 | v&0xFFFF0000>>16
   152	                }
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        return func(f float64) ([]byte, error) {
   156	                v := fun(f)
   157	                b := make([]byte, 2*length)
   158	
   159	                switch length {
   160	                case 1:
   161	                        binary.BigEndian.PutUint16(b[:], uint16(v))
   162	                case 2:
   163	                        binary.BigEndian.PutUint32(b[:], uint32(v))
   164	                case 4:
   165	                        binary.BigEndian.PutUint64(b[:], v)
   166	                default:
   167	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid register length: %d", length)
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                return b, nil
   171	        }, nil
   172	}
   173	
   174	func (r Register) EncodeFunc() (func(float64) ([]byte, error), error) {
   175	        enc := strings.ToLower(r.encoding())
   176	
   177	        switch {
   178	        case strings.HasPrefix(enc, "bool"):
   179	                fallthrough
   180	
   181	        case strings.HasPrefix(enc, "int"):
   182	                return r.encodeToBytes(func(v float64) uint64 {
   183	                        return uint64(int64(v))
   184	                })
   185	
   186	        case strings.HasPrefix(enc, "uint"):
   187	                return r.encodeToBytes(func(v float64) uint64 {
   188	                        return uint64(v)
   189	                })
   190	
   191	        case strings.HasPrefix(enc, "float") || strings.HasPrefix(enc, "ieee754"):
   192	                length, err := r.Length()
   193	                if err != nil {
   194	                        return nil, err
   195	                }
   196	
   197	                switch length {
   198	                case 2:
   199	                        return r.encodeToBytes(func(v float64) uint64 {
   200	                                return uint64(math.Float32bits(float32(v)))
   201	                        })
   202	
   203	                case 4:
   204	                        return r.encodeToBytes(func(v float64) uint64 {
   205	                                return math.Float64bits(v)
   206	                        })
   207	
   208	                default:
   209	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid register length: %d", length)
   210	                }
   211	
   212	        default:
   213	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid register encoding: %s", r.encoding())
   214	        }
   215	}
   216	
   217	type RegisterOperation struct {
   218	        FuncCode uint8
   219	        Addr     uint16
   220	        Length   uint16
   221	}
   222	
   223	// Operation creates a modbus operation from a register definition
   224	func (r Register) Operation() (RegisterOperation, error) {
   225	        len, err := r.Length()
   226	        if err != nil {
   227	                return RegisterOperation{}, err
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        fc, err := r.FuncCode()
   231	        if err != nil {
   232	                return RegisterOperation{}, err
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        op := RegisterOperation{
   236	                Addr:     r.Address,
   237	                Length:   len,
   238	                FuncCode: fc,
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        return op, nil
   242	}
   243	
   244	// asFloat64 creates a function that returns numerics vales as float64
   245	func asFloat64[T constraints.Signed | constraints.Unsigned | constraints.Float](f func([]byte) T) func([]byte) float64 {
   246	        return func(v []byte) float64 {
   247	                res := float64(f(v))
   248	                if math.IsNaN(res) || math.IsInf(res, 0) {
   249	                        res = 0
   250	                }
   251	                return res
   252	        }
   253	}

// interprets it according to decode.
func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
	switch decode {
	case "int32be":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(int32(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))), nil
	case "uint32be":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:])), nil
	case "int16be":
		if len(payload) < offset+2 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(int16(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:]))), nil
	case "uint16be":
		if len(payload) < offset+2 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
	}
	return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode type: %s", decode)
}' --new_str '// decodeAt extracts an integer at the given byte offset of payload and
// interprets it according to decode.
func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
	switch decode {
	case "int32be":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(int32(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))), nil
	case "uint32be":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:])), nil
	case "int16be":
		if len(payload) < offset+2 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(int16(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:]))), nil
	case "uint16be":
		if len(payload) < offset+2 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
	case "float32":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32 at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))
		if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
			return 0, nil
		}
		return float64(v), nil
	case "float32s":
		if len(payload) < offset+4 {
			return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32s at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
		}
		// word-swapped: swap the two 16-bit words, then interpret as big-endian
		b := make([]byte, 4)
		b[0], b[1] = payload[offset+2], payload[offset+3]
		b[2], b[3] = payload[offset], payload[offset+1]
		v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
		if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
			return 0, nil
		}
		return float64(v), nil
	}
	return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode type: %s", decode)
}'

   184	// interprets it according to decode.
   185	func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
   186	        switch decode {
   187	        case "int32be":
   188	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   189	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   190	                }
   191	                return float64(int32(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))), nil
   192	        case "uint32be":
   193	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   194	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   195	                }
   196	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:])), nil
   197	        case "int16be":
   198	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   199	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   200	                }
   201	                return float64(int16(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:]))), nil
   202	        case "uint16be":
   203	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   204	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   205	                }
   206	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
   207	        case "float32":
   208	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   209	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32 at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   210	                }
   211	                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))
   212	                if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
   213	                        return 0, nil
   214	                }
   215	                return float64(v), nil
   216	        case "float32s":
   217	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   218	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32s at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   219	                }
   220	                // word-swapped: swap the two 16-bit words, then interpret as big-endian
   221	                b := make([]byte, 4)
   222	                b[0], b[1] = payload[offset+2], payload[offset+3]
   223	                b[2], b[3] = payload[offset], payload[offset+1]
   224	                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
   225	                if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
   226	                        return 0, nil
   227	                }
   228	                return float64(v), nil
   229	        }
   230	        return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode type: %s", decode)
   231	}
   232	
   233	// modbusCRC16 computes the Modbus CRC-16 (little-endian byte order).
   234	func modbusCRC16(data []byte) []byte {
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

All tests pass. Now let me also write a quick script to explicitly test the float32 decode:







🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_float32.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"encoding/binary"
	"fmt"
	"math"
)

func main() {
	// Test float32 encode/decode round-trip
	// Example: energy value 6085.3 kWh
	// The goodwe-hybrid template uses: decode: float32, scale: 0.001
	// So the register holds the value in Wh as a float32
	
	// Let's encode a test value
	val := float32(6085300.0) // 6085.3 kWh = 6085300 Wh
	bits := math.Float32bits(val)
	
	b := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.BigEndian.PutUint32(b, bits)
	fmt.Printf("Big-endian float32 of %f: %x\n", val, b)
	
	// Decode it back
	decoded := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
	fmt.Printf("Decoded: %f\n", decoded)
	fmt.Printf("With scale 0.001: %f\n", float64(decoded) * 0.001)
	
	// Also test word-swapped decode
	bs := make([]byte, 4)
	bs[0], bs[1] = b[2], b[3]
	bs[2], bs[3] = b[0], b[1]
	decodedS := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(bs))
	fmt.Printf("Swapped decoded: %f\n", decodedS)
	fmt.Printf("With scale 0.001: %f\n", float64(decodedS) * 0.001)
	
	// Test NaN handling
	nanBytes := []byte{0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x7f} // NaN
	v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(nanBytes))
	fmt.Printf("NaN case: v=%f, IsNaN=%v\n", v, math.IsNaN(float64(v)))
	
	// Test Inf
	infBytes := []byte{0x7f, 0x80, 0x00, 0x00} // +Inf
	v2 := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(infBytes))
	fmt.Printf("Inf case: v=%f, IsInf=%v\n", v2, math.IsInf(float64(v2), 0))
}
EOF

2026-05-29 22:39:20,838 - INFO - swea-agent-evcc-io__evcc-28765 - 💭 THOUGHT
The float32 decode/encode round-trip works correctly. Now let me write a comprehensive test that simulates the actual use case from the template - using `decode: float32` with `scale: 0.001` for energy:









🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_aa55udp_float32.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"encoding/binary"
	"fmt"
	"math"
)

// Simulate decodeAt for float32
func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
	switch decode {
	case "float32":
		v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))
		if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
			return 0, nil
		}
		return float64(v), nil
	case "float32s":
		b := make([]byte, 4)
		b[0], b[1] = payload[offset+2], payload[offset+3]
		b[2], b[3] = payload[offset], payload[offset+1]
		v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
		if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
			return 0, nil
		}
		return float64(v), nil
	}
	return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode: %s", decode)
}

func main() {
	// Test scenario: register 36017 (E-Total-Buy) from GoodWe ET inverter
	// The template uses decode: float32, scale: 0.001
	// The register holds energy in Wh as a 32-bit float
	
	// Example: 6085.3 kWh = 6085300 Wh
	// As float32: 0x4ab9b568
	
	payload := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.BigEndian.PutUint32(payload, math.Float32bits(6085300.0))
	
	fmt.Printf("Payload: %x\n", payload)
	
	v, err := decodeAt(payload, 0, "float32")
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("Decoded value: %f\n", v)
		fmt.Printf("With scale 0.001: %f\n", v * 0.001)
	}
	
	// Test edge cases: value = 0
	payload0 := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.BigEndian.PutUint32(payload0, math.Float32bits(0.0))
	v0, _ := decodeAt(payload0, 0, "float32")
	fmt.Printf("Zero: %f\n", v0)
	
	// Test negative (should not happen for energy, but good to verify)
	payloadNeg := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.BigEndian.PutUint32(payloadNeg, math.Float32bits(-100.5))
	vNeg, _ := decodeAt(payloadNeg, 0, "float32")
	fmt.Printf("Negative: %f\n", vNeg)
	
	fmt.Println("All float32 tests passed!")
}
EOF
GOTOOLCHAIN=auto go run /tmp/test_aa55udp_float32.go

    17	// AA55UDP implements the GoodWe WiFi AA55-over-UDP wire protocol as a generic
    18	// evcc source plugin.
    19	//
    20	// The inverter speaks a simple request/response protocol over UDP port 8899:
    21	//
    22	//      Request:  [6-byte Modbus PDU body] [Modbus CRC-16, little-endian]
    23	//      Response: AA 55 [src] 03 [byteCount] [payload…] [CRC]
    24	//
    25	// src varies by inverter family (0x7F for DT/DNS, 0xF7 for ET/EH/BT/BH);
    26	// only the AA 55 magic bytes and function code 0x03 are validated.
    27	//
    28	// Each instance reads exactly one value from one register (or register pair
    29	// for 32-bit values), matching how Modbus source plugins work.  The PDU is
    30	// constructed from register and count; the decoded value is always at offset 0
    31	// of the response payload.
    32	type AA55UDP struct {
    33	        log    *util.Logger
    34	        conn   *net.UDPConn
    35	        pdu    []byte // 6-byte PDU body, no CRC
    36	        decode string // int32be | uint32be | int16be | uint16be
    37	        scale  float64
    38	}
    39	
    40	func init() {
    41	        registry.AddCtx("aa55udp", NewAA55UDPFromConfig)
    42	}
    43	
    44	// NewAA55UDPFromConfig creates an AA55UDP plugin from a source block:
    45	//
    46	//      source:   aa55udp
    47	//      host:     192.168.1.26   # inverter IP; port 8899 is always used
    48	//      register: 30127          # Modbus register address (0-based, uint16)
    49	//      count:    2              # number of registers to read (1=U16, 2=S32/U32)
    50	//      decode:   int32be        # int32be | uint32be | int16be | uint16be
    51	//      scale:    1.0            # optional multiplier (default 1.0)
    52	func NewAA55UDPFromConfig(_ context.Context, other map[string]interface{}) (Plugin, error) {
    53	        cc := struct {
    54	                Host     string  `mapstructure:"host"`
    55	                Register uint16  `mapstructure:"register"`
    56	                Count    uint16  `mapstructure:"count"`
    57	                Decode   string  `mapstructure:"decode"`
    58	                Scale    float64 `mapstructure:"scale"`
    59	        }{
    60	                Count: 2,
    61	                Scale: 1.0,
    62	        }
    63	        if err := util.DecodeOther(other, &cc); err != nil {
    64	                return nil, err
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        if cc.Count == 0 {
    68	                return nil, errors.New("aa55udp: count must be ≥ 1")
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        switch cc.Decode {
    72	        case "int32be", "uint32be", "int16be", "uint16be", "float32", "float32s":
    73	        default:
    74	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: unsupported decode %q (want int32be|uint32be|int16be|uint16be|float32|float32s)", cc.Decode)
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        pdu := buildPDU(cc.Register, cc.Count)
    78	
    79	        addr, err := net.ResolveUDPAddr("udp4", net.JoinHostPort(cc.Host, "8899"))
    80	        if err != nil {
    81	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: resolve %s: %w", cc.Host, err)
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        conn, err := net.DialUDP("udp4", nil, addr)
    85	        if err != nil {
    86	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: dial %s: %w", cc.Host, err)
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        return &AA55UDP{
    90	                log:    util.NewLogger("aa55udp"),
    91	                conn:   conn,
    92	                pdu:    pdu,
    93	                decode: cc.Decode,
    94	                scale:  cc.Scale,
    95	        }, nil
    96	}
    97	
    98	// FloatGetter implements the evcc Plugin interface.
    99	func (p *AA55UDP) FloatGetter() (func() (float64, error), error) {
   100	        return p.query, nil
   101	}
   102	
   103	// query sends the PDU and returns the decoded, scaled value at offset 0 of the
   104	// response payload.
   105	func (p *AA55UDP) query() (float64, error) {
   106	        packet := append(p.pdu, modbusCRC16(p.pdu)...)
   107	
   108	        if _, err := p.conn.Write(packet); err != nil {
   109	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp write: %w", err)
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if err := p.conn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(4 * time.Second)); err != nil {
   113	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp deadline: %w", err)
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        buf := make([]byte, 512)
   117	        n, err := p.conn.Read(buf)
   118	        if err != nil {
   119	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp read: %w", err)
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        payload, err := stripAA55Header(buf[:n])
   123	        if err != nil {
   124	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: %w", err)
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        v, err := decodeAt(payload, 0, p.decode)
   128	        if err != nil {
   129	                return 0, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: %w", err)
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        return v * p.scale, nil
   133	}
   134	
   135	// aa55InverterAddr is the target address byte used in all AA55 request PDUs.
   136	// The GoodWe WiFi module always uses 0x7F as the inverter target address,
   137	// regardless of inverter family. The family only affects the source byte in
   138	// responses (0x7F for DT/DNS, 0xF7 for ET/EH/BT/BH).
   139	const aa55InverterAddr = 0x7F
   140	
   141	// aa55ReadFunc is the Modbus function code for READ HOLDING REGISTERS.
   142	const aa55ReadFunc = 0x03
   143	
   144	// buildPDU constructs the 6-byte Modbus PDU body for a READ HOLDING REGISTERS
   145	// request targeting the GoodWe WiFi module.
   146	func buildPDU(register, count uint16) []byte {
   147	        return []byte{
   148	                aa55InverterAddr, aa55ReadFunc,
   149	                byte(register >> 8), byte(register),
   150	                byte(count >> 8), byte(count),
   151	        }
   152	}
   153	
   154	// parsePDUHex decodes a hex string (spaces allowed) into exactly 6 bytes.
   155	// Kept for use in tests.
   156	func parsePDUHex(s string) ([]byte, error) {
   157	        clean := strings.ReplaceAll(s, " ", "")
   158	        b, err := hex.DecodeString(clean)
   159	        if err != nil {
   160	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: invalid pdu %q: %w", s, err)
   161	        }
   162	        if len(b) != 6 {
   163	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("aa55udp: pdu must be 6 bytes, got %d", len(b))
   164	        }
   165	        return b, nil
   166	}
   167	
   168	// stripAA55Header validates the AA55 response frame and returns the bare
   169	// payload (without the 5-byte header and trailing 2-byte CRC).
   170	// buf[2] is the inverter source address and varies by family — only the
   171	// AA 55 magic bytes and function code 0x03 are validated.
   172	func stripAA55Header(buf []byte) ([]byte, error) {
   173	        if len(buf) < 6 || buf[0] != 0xAA || buf[1] != 0x55 || buf[3] != 0x03 {
   174	                return nil, errors.New("invalid response header")
   175	        }
   176	        byteCount := int(buf[4])
   177	        if len(buf) < 5+byteCount+2 {
   178	                return nil, errors.New("short response")
   179	        }
   180	        return buf[5 : 5+byteCount], nil
   181	}
   182	
   183	// decodeAt extracts an integer at the given byte offset of payload and
   184	// interprets it according to decode.
   185	func decodeAt(payload []byte, offset int, decode string) (float64, error) {
   186	        switch decode {
   187	        case "int32be":
   188	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   189	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   190	                }
   191	                return float64(int32(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))), nil
   192	        case "uint32be":
   193	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   194	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint32be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   195	                }
   196	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:])), nil
   197	        case "int16be":
   198	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   199	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for int16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   200	                }
   201	                return float64(int16(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:]))), nil
   202	        case "uint16be":
   203	                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
   204	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   205	                }
   206	                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
   207	        case "float32":
   208	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   209	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32 at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   210	                }
   211	                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))
   212	                if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
   213	                        return 0, nil
   214	                }
   215	                return float64(v), nil
   216	        case "float32s":
   217	                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
   218	                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32s at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
   219	                }
   220	                // word-swapped: swap the two 16-bit words, then interpret as big-endian
   221	                b := make([]byte, 4)
   222	                b[0], b[1] = payload[offset+2], payload[offset+3]
   223	                b[2], b[3] = payload[offset], payload[offset+1]
   224	                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
   225	                if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
   226	                        return 0, nil
   227	                }
   228	                return float64(v), nil
   229	        }
   230	        return 0, fmt.Errorf("unknown decode type: %s", decode)
   231	}
   232	
   233	// modbusCRC16 computes the Modbus CRC-16 (little-endian byte order).
   234	func modbusCRC16(data []byte) []byte {
   235	        crc := uint16(0xFFFF)
   236	        for _, b := range data {
   237	                crc ^= uint16(b)
   238	                for i := 0; i < 8; i++ {
   239	                        if crc&0x0001 != 0 {
   240	                                crc = (crc >> 1) ^ 0xA001
   241	                        } else {
   242	                                crc >>= 1
   243	                        }
   244	                }
   245	        }
   246	        return []byte{byte(crc & 0xFF), byte(crc >> 8)}
   247	}

+                }

+                if len(payload) < offset+2 {
+                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for uint16be at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
+                }
+                return float64(binary.BigEndian.Uint16(payload[offset:])), nil
+        case "float32":
+                if len(payload) < offset+4 {
+                        return 0, fmt.Errorf("payload too short for float32 at offset %d (len=%d)", offset, len(payload))
+                }
+                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(payload[offset:]))

+                b[2], b[3] = payload[offset], payload[offset+1]
+                v := math.Float32frombits(binary.BigEndian.Uint32(b))
+                if math.IsNaN(float64(v)) || math.IsInf(float64(v), 0) {
+                        return 0, nil
+                }
+                return float64(v), nil
+        }

 // modbusCRC16 computes the Modbus CRC-16 (little-endian byte order).
 func modbusCRC16(data []byte) []byte {

-	for _, b := range data {
-		crc ^= uint16(b)

+        crc := uint16(0xFFFF)
+        for _, b := range data {
+                crc ^= uint16(b)
+                for i := 0; i < 8; i++ {
+                        if crc&0x0001 != 0 {
+                                crc = (crc >> 1) ^ 0xA001
+                        } else {
+                                crc >>= 1
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        return []byte{byte(crc & 0xFF), byte(crc >> 8)}
